Key:        LU-1146
Summary:    update copyright for all WC modified files in master before 2.2 release
Link:       https://jira.whamcloud.com/browse/LU-1146
Type:       Improvement
Priority:   Minor
Status:     Resolved
Resolution: Fixed
Assignee:   Andreas Dilger
Reporter:   Andreas Dilger
Created:    Tue, 28 Feb 2012 05:40:51 +0000
Updated:    Wed, 2 May 2012 15:37:32 +0000
Resolved:   Thu, 5 Apr 2012 19:53:36 +0000

--- Description ---
The copyright message for all files modified by Whamcloud for the 2.2 release should be updated with a copyright statement following the Oracle copyright at the start of each file:

 * Copyright (c) 2012, Whamcloud, Inc.

If the file was modified in 2011 and 2012 it should read:

 * Copyright (c) 2011, 2012, Whamcloud, Inc.

It is likely that build/updatecw.sh can be modified to add new copyright messages.  Currently, it can only replace them.

--- Comment (adilger, Thu, 5 Apr 2012 19:53:36 +0000) ---
The actual copyright messages were fixed for 2.2.0, and the script was landed for 2.3.0.

One minor side-effect of the mass copyright updates is that some files will show as being modified by Whamcloud in 2012 due to the copyright update itself, even though the copyright was changed to reflect an update in 2011.  That is something to be addressed if this script is being run en-masse again.
